  <script>
   function LazyLoadImages() {
    var config = {
      rootMargin: '50px 0px',
      threshold: 0.01
    };
    var observer;

    var lazyElements = [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll(".lazy"));
    var lazyDivs = [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('.embedResponsiveItem.hide'));

    function removeLazy(target) {
      target.classList.remove("lazy");
    }

    function lazyLoadImage(elm, cb) {
      if(elm.dataset && elm.dataset.src) {
        elm.src = elm.dataset.src;
      }

      if(elm.dataset && elm.dataset.srcset) {
        elm.srcset = elm.dataset.srcset
      }

      elm.onload = function () {
        elm.classList.remove('blur');
        if (typeof cb === "function") {
            cb();
        }
      }
    }

    function lazyLoadPicture(target) {
      Array.from(target.children).forEach(function(elm) {
        lazyLoadImage(elm, removeLazy.bind(null, target));
      });
    }

    function lazyLoadDiv(elm) {
      elm.style.backgroundImage = 'url("'+ elm.dataset.imgscr +'")';
      elm.classList.remove('hide', 'blur');
    }

    function onIntersection(entries) {
      entries.forEach(function(entry) {
        if(entry.isIntersecting) {
          observer.unobserve(entry.target);

          if(entry.target.tagName === 'PICTURE') {
            lazyLoadPicture(entry.target);
          }

          if(entry.target.tagName === 'IMG') {
            lazyLoadImage(entry.target, removeLazy.bind(null, entry.target));
          }

          if(entry.target.tagName === 'DIV') {
            lazyLoadDiv(entry.target);
          }
        }
      });
    }

    if (!('IntersectionObserver' in window)) {
      lazyElements.forEach(function(target) {
        if(target.tagName === 'PICTURE') {
          lazyLoadPicture(target);
        }

        if(target.tagName === 'IMG') {
          lazyLoadImage(target);
        }
      });
      lazyDivs.forEach(function(div) { lazyLoadDiv(div); });
    } else {
      observer = new IntersectionObserver(onIntersection, config);
      lazyElements.forEach(function(image) { observer.observe(image) });
    }
  }

  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    LazyLoadImages();
  });
  </script>
